## Opcodes

```
  0: 0x0479 [0x6E] EventEntity uses emote 7*
  1: 0x0480 [0x99] Wait for EventEntity animation to complete
  2: 0x0485 [0x1C] WAIT(150* ticks)
  3: 0x0488 [0x32] ExtData[1]->MainSpeed = 13* * 0.1
  4: 0x048B [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: EventEntity moves to X=-399.449*, Z=389.172*, Y=-201.624*
  5: 0x0493 [0x1F] MOVE_ENTITY: Update entity position (mode=1)
  6: 0x0495 [0x00] END_REQSTACK()
```
